deprecated\\n\\n## Integration with API Server\\n\\nThe complete migration path:\\n1. User submits v1beta1 Ingress with optional pathType\\n2. v1beta1 defaults plugin adds ImplementationSpecific default\\n3. Conversion layer converts to internal representation\\n4.
